\end{equation}
Therefore we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \partial_t w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u^c \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w^c \partial_z w - St \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z u \partial_r \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i + 2 \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^f} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_r \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}, \tag{5.9}
\end{align}
We now consider the last integral in the right hand side of the equation above
\begin{align}
\int_{\partial \Omega} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n} &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,1}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4, \tag{5.10}
\end{align}
where $\partial \Omega^{1}$ is the free surface, $\partial \Omega^{2}$ is the solid surface, and $\partial \Omega^{3}$ is the axis of symmetry. For the free surface we have equation (2.10), which states
\begin{equation}
\mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^1 = -p^g \mathbf{n}^1 - \frac{\nabla^s \cdot [\sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)]}{\ca}, \tag{5.11}
\end{equation}
and therefore
\begin{equation}
\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^1 = -\phi_i p^g \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{n}^1 - \frac{1}{\ca} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \nabla^s \cdot [\sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)]. \tag{5.12}
\end{equation}
Now, we have the following surface vector calculus identity
\begin{equation}
\nabla^s \cdot (\mathbf{x} \cdot \mathbf{A}) = \mathbf{A} : \nabla^s \mathbf{x} + \mathbf{x} \cdot \nabla^s \cdot \mathbf{A}, \tag{5.13}
\end{equation}
taking $\mathbf{x} = \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z$ and $\mathbf{A} = \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)$, we have
\begin{equation}
\nabla^s \cdot (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)) = \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1) : \nabla^s (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z) + \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \nabla^s \cdot \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1), \tag{5.14}
\end{equation}
which yields
\begin{equation}
-\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \nabla^s \cdot \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1) = -\nabla^s \cdot (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)) + \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1) : \nabla^s (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z). \tag{5.15}
\end{equation}
In this 1D surface case, we have
\begin{equation}
\nabla^s (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z) = \begin{bmatrix} 0 & \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \\ 0 & \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \end{bmatrix}, \tag{5.16}
\end{equation}
and therefore
\begin{equation}
(\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1) : \nabla^s (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z) = \begin{bmatrix} 1 - n_z^1 n_z^1 & -n_z^1 n_z^1 \\ -n_z^1 n_z^1 & 1 - n_z^1 n_z^1 \end{bmatrix} : \begin{bmatrix} 0 & \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \\ 0 & \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \end{bmatrix} = \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1, \tag{5.17}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
(\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1) : \nabla^s (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z) = \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 - \partial_s \phi_i n_z^1 (t^1 \cdot \mathbf{n}^1) = \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1. \tag{5.18}
\end{equation}
We therefore have in equation (5.15)
\begin{equation}
-\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \nabla^s \cdot \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1) = -\nabla^s \cdot (\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \sigma^1 (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)) + \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1. \tag{5.19}
\end{equation}
Taking equation (5.19) into (5.12) and the result of that into (5.10) and finally taking into (5.9) we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \partial_t w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u^c \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w^c \partial_z w - St \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_r \phi_i + 2 \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i - \int_{\partial \Omega^1} \phi_i p^g \mathbf{e}_z \cdot n^1 - \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^1} \nabla^s \cdot (\sigma^1 \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1)) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^1} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^2} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^3} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^3 + \int_{\partial \Omega^4} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^4. \tag{5.20}
\end{align}
Using the surface divergence theorem and the definition of the surface divergence for a 1D surface, we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \partial_t w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u^c \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w^c \partial_z w - St \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_r \phi_i + 2 \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i - \int_{\partial \Omega^1} \phi_i p^g n_z^1 + \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{C_1} \sigma^1 \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot m^1 + \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^1} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^2} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^3} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^3 + \int_{\partial \Omega^4} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^4, \tag{5.21}
\end{align}
where $C_1$ is actually the two points bounding the free surface, and $m^1$ is the vector that is tangent to the free surface, normal to the separatrix line or symmetry axis (accordingly) and points into the far-field free surface. Therefore we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \partial_t w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u^c \partial_r w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w^c \partial_z w \nonumber\\
&\quad - St \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z u \partial_r \phi_i + 2 \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i - \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i - \int_{\partial \Omega^1} p^g \phi_i n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{\sigma^1(r_{j1},z_{j1}) \phi_i(r_{j1},z_{j1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{j1},z_{j1})}{\ca} + \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^1} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^2} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^3} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^3 + \int_{\partial \Omega^4} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot n^4, \tag{5.22}
\end{align}
where $m^{1,n}(r_{j1},z_{j1})$ is tangent to the near-field portion of the free surface. This choice is important as it prevents formation of a corner on the free surface when solving the simulations.
We consider now the term
\begin{equation}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2. \tag{5.23}
\end{equation}
We have
\begin{align}
\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 &= \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \underbrace{(\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^2 \mathbf{n}^2) \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2}_{\be (\mathbf{u} - \mathbf{u}^s) \cdot (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^2 \mathbf{n}^2) - \frac{1}{2\ca} \nabla^2 \sigma^2} + \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \underbrace{(\mathbf{n}^2 \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2)}_{\lambda^2} \mathbf{n}^2, \tag{5.24}
\end{align}
where $\lambda^2$ is the normal stress on surface 2 and we have used the GNSC [2.53], and therefore
\begin{align}
\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 &= \be \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot (\mathbf{u} \cdot \mathbf{t}^2) \mathbf{t}^2 - \be \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot (\mathbf{u}^s \cdot \mathbf{t}^2) \mathbf{t}^2 - \frac{1}{2\ca} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \nabla^2 \sigma^2 + \lambda^2 \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{n}^2, \tag{5.25}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 &= \be \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot (u t_r^2 + w t_z^2) \mathbf{t}^2 - \be \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot (u^s t_r^2 + w^s t_z^2) \mathbf{t}^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \phi_i (\partial_s \sigma^2) \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{t}^2 + \lambda^2 \phi_i n_z^2, \tag{5.26}
\end{align}
where we have used that $\nabla^2 \sigma^2 = \partial_s \sigma^2 \mathbf{t}^2$ (with $\mathbf{t}^2$ pointing in the direction of increasing arc-length $s$). Equivalently, we have
\begin{align}
\phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 &= \be \phi_i u t_r^2 t_z^2 + \be \phi_i w t_z^2 t_z^2 - \be \phi_i u^s t_r^2 t_z^2 - \be \phi_i w^s t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \sigma^2 + \lambda^2 \phi_i n_z^2. \tag{5.27}
\end{align}
Consequently we have
\begin{align}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 &= \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i u t_r^2 t_z^2 + \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i w t_z^2 t_z^2 - \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i u^s t_r^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i w^s t_z^2 t_z^2 - \frac{1}{2\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \sigma^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,1}} \lambda^2 \phi_i n_z^2. \tag{5.28}
\end{align}
Similarly, we have for the term
\begin{align}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3, \quad
\mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3 = \mathbf{n}^3 \underbrace{\mathbf{n}^3 \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3}_{\lambda^3} + \underbrace{(\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^3 \mathbf{n}^3) \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3}_{\gamma^3 \mathbf{t}^3}, \tag{5.30}
\end{align}
where $\lambda^3$ is the normal stress on surface 3 and $\gamma^3$ is the tangential stress on surface 3. We therefore have
\begin{equation}
\mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3 = \lambda^3 \mathbf{n}^3 + \gamma^3 \mathbf{t}^3. \tag{5.31}
\end{equation}
Consequently we have
\begin{equation}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3 = \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_i \lambda^3 \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{n}^3 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_i \gamma^3 \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{t}^3, \tag{5.32}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^3 = \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \lambda^3 n_z^3 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \gamma^3 t_z^3 \phi_i. \tag{5.33}
\end{equation}
Finally, for the term
\begin{equation}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4, \quad
\mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4 = \mathbf{n}^4 \underbrace{\mathbf{n}^4 \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4}_{\lambda^4} + \underbrace{(\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^4 \mathbf{n}^4) \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4}_{\gamma^4 \mathbf{t}^4}, \tag{5.35}
\end{equation}
where $\lambda^4$ is the normal stress on surface 4 and $\gamma^4$ is the tangential stress on surface 4. We therefore have
\begin{equation}
\mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4 = \lambda^4 \mathbf{n}^4 + \gamma^4 \mathbf{t}^4. \tag{5.36}
\end{equation}
Consequently we have
\begin{equation}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4 = \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_i \lambda^4 \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{n}^4 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_i \gamma^4 \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{t}^4, \tag{5.37}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_i \mathbf{e}_z \cdot \mathbf{P} \cdot \mathbf{n}^4 = \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \lambda^4 n_z^4 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \gamma^4 t_z^4 \phi_i. \tag{5.38}
\end{equation}
Taking (5.28) and (5.33) into (5.22) we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \partial_t w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u^c \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w^c \partial_z w - St \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z u \partial_r \phi_i + 2 \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i p^g n_z^1 + \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} + \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 + \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i u t_r^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i w t_z^2 t_z^2 - \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i u^s t_r^2 t_z^2 - \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i w^s t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \sigma^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \lambda^2 \phi_i n_z^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \lambda^3 n_z^3 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \gamma^3 t_z^3 \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \lambda^4 n_z^4 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \gamma^4 t_z^4 \phi_i, \tag{5.39}
\end{align}
We recall approximations (4.52)-(4.55) and substitute them into (5.39) obtaining
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \frac{3w(t_n) - 4w(t_{n-1}) + w(t_{n-2})}{2\dt} + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad + Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \frac{3r^c(t_n) - 4r^c(t_{n-1}) + r^c(t_{n-2})}{2\dt} \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \frac{3z^c(t_n) - 4z^c(t_{n-1}) + z^c(t_{n-2})}{2\dt} \partial_z w - St \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \bar{g}_z \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_r \phi_i + 2 \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i - \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i p^g n_z^1 + \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J^1},z_{J^1}) \phi_i(r_{J^1},z_{J^1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J^1},z_{J^1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} + \frac{1}{\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i u t_r^2 t_z^2 + \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i w t_z^2 t_z^2 - \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i u^s t_r^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \be \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i w^s t_z^2 t_z^2 - \frac{1}{2\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \sigma^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \lambda^2 \phi_i n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \lambda^3 n_z^3 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \gamma^3 t_z^3 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \lambda^4 n_z^4 \phi_i + \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \gamma^4 t_z^4 \phi_i, \tag{5.40}
\end{align}
and multiplying (5.40) by $2\dt/3$ we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w - \frac{4Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w(t_{n-1}) + \frac{Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w(t_{n-2}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i u \partial_r w + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i w \partial_z w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i r^c \partial_r w + \frac{4Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i r^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_r w - \frac{Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i r^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_r w \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i z^c \partial_z w + \frac{4Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i z^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_z w - \frac{Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i z^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_z w \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r w \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z u \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{4\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z w \partial_z \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} p \partial_z \phi_i - \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i p^g n_z^1 + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a) + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i u t_r^2 t_z^2 + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i w t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i u^s t_r^2 t_z^2 - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i w^s t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \sigma^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \lambda^2 \phi_i n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \lambda^3 n_z^3 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \gamma^3 t_z^3 \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \lambda^4 n_z^4 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \gamma^4 t_z^4 \phi_i, \tag{5.41}
\end{align}
where time dependent function whose time argument is not indicated are evaluated at time $t_n$.
We now substitute approximations (4.66)-(4.80) into (5.41) and define
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j - \frac{4Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-1}) \phi_j + \frac{Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-2}) \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} u_k \phi_k \right) \partial_r \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} w_k \phi_k \right) \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c \phi_k \right) \partial_r \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) + \frac{4Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-1}) \phi_k \right) \partial_r \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-2}) \phi_k \right) \partial_r \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c \phi_k \right) \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) + \frac{4Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-1}) \phi_k \right) \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \left( \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-2}) \phi_k \right) \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) - \frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j \right) \partial_r \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \partial_z \phi_i - \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_p} p_j \psi_j \right) \partial_z \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{p}_j^g \phi_j^1 \right) n_z^1 + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a) + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^1 \phi_j^1 \right) t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_r^2 t_z^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j \right) + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 t_z^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{u}_j^s \phi_j \right) t_r^2 t_z^2 - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{w}_j^s \phi_j \right) t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^2 \phi_j^2 \right) + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^2 \phi_j \right) \phi_i n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^3 \phi_j \right) n_z^3 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^3 \phi_j \right) t_z^3 \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^4 \phi_j \right) n_z^4 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^4 \phi_j \right) t_z^4 \phi_i, \tag{5.42}
\end{align}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0} &= Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_j - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_j + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} u_k \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} w_k \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j - Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r \phi_j \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z \phi_j \partial_r \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z \phi_j \partial_z \phi_i - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_p} p_j \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_j \partial_z \phi_i, \tag{5.45}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} &= -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{p}_j^g \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i \phi_j^1 n_z^1 + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1}(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a) + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^1 \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_j^1 t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_i, \tag{5.46}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_r^2 t_z^2 \phi_j + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 t_z^2 \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{u}_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i \phi_j t_r^2 t_z^2 - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{w}_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i \phi_j t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \phi_j^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_j \phi_i n_z^2, \tag{5.47}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,3} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^3 \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_j n_z^3 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^3 \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} t_z^3 \phi_j \phi_i, \tag{5.48}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,4} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^4 \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_j n_z^4 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^4 \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} t_z^4 \phi_j \phi_i. \tag{5.49}
\end{align}
Re-arranging terms we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0} &= -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \hat{g}_z + Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_j - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_j + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_r \phi_j \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z \phi_j \partial_r \phi_i \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega^f} \partial_z \phi_j \partial_z \phi_i + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} u_k \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} w_k \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j - Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega^f} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_p} p_j \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_j \partial_z \phi_i, \tag{5.50}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} &= \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1}(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^1 \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_j^1 t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_i - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{p}_j^g \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i \phi_j^1 n_z^1, \tag{5.51}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_r^2 t_z^2 \phi_j + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 t_z^2 \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{u}_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i \phi_j t_r^2 t_z^2 - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{w}_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i \phi_j t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \phi_j^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_j \phi_i n_z^2, \tag{5.52}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,3} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^3 \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} \phi_j n_z^3 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^3 \int_{\partial \Omega^{3}} t_z^3 \phi_j \phi_i, \tag{5.53}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,4} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^4 \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} \phi_j n_z^4 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^4 \int_{\partial \Omega^{4}} t_z^4 \phi_j \phi_i. \tag{5.54}
\end{align}
We now use the same triangular domain partition and proceed to decompose the integrals above in a sum of integrals over each element. The boundary integrals are in turn converted into a sum of integrals over line elements on the boundary, i.e. those portions of the boundary of the triangular elements that lie on the domain boundary $\partial \Omega$. This yields
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{M}_i^z = \underbrace{\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0a} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,0b} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,0c} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,0d} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,2} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,3} + \mathcal{M}_i^{z,4}}_{\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0}}, \tag{5.55}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0a} = \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \left[ -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \hat{g}_z \right], \tag{5.56}
\end{equation}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0b} &= \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \Bigg[ Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_j - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_j + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_r \phi_j \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_j \partial_r \phi_i + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_j \partial_z \phi_i \Bigg], \tag{5.57}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0c} &= \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} u_k \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} w_k \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} r_k^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_r \phi_j - Re \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \sum_{k=1}^{n_v} z_k^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_i \phi_k \partial_z \phi_j \Bigg], \tag{5.58}
\end{align}
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0d} = \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \left[ -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_p} p_j \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_j \partial_z \phi_i \right], \tag{5.59}
\end{equation}
and, as before,
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} &= \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_{j1},z_{j1}) \phi_i(r_{j1},z_{j1}) m_z^{1}(r_{j1},z_{j1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{e_1=1}^{n_{el}^1} \left[ \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^1 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_j^1 t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_i - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{p}_j^g \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i \phi_j^1 n_z^1 \right], \tag{5.60}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,2} &= \sum_{e_2=1}^{n_{el}^2} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_i t_r^2 t_z^2 \phi_j + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_i t_z^2 t_z^2 \phi_j \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{u}_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_i t_r^2 t_z^2 - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{w}_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_i \phi_j t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\sigma}_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_i t_z^2 \partial_s \phi_j^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_j \phi_i n_z^2 \Bigg], \tag{5.61}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,3} = \sum_{e_3=1}^{n_{el}^3} \left[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} \phi_j n_z^3 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} t_z^3 \phi_j \phi_i \right], \tag{5.62}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,4} = \sum_{e_4=1}^{n_{el}^4} \left[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\lambda}_j^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} \phi_j n_z^4 \phi_i + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \tilde{\gamma}_j^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} t_z^4 \phi_j \phi_i \right]; \tag{5.63}
\end{align}
where $\Omega_e$ is the curved-sided triangular portion of the domain that defines element $e$ and $\partial \Omega_{e_k}$ is the portion of the boundary $\partial \Omega_k$ that lies on the line element $e_k$. We notice that the vast majority of the terms that are added in the sum on each element is identically null. This is, of course, because each one of the basis functions $\phi_i$ and $\psi_i$ is chosen so that they are only supported on the elements that contain node $i$. Therefore, a more efficient way to express this sums is to resort to local node numbering. That is to say, when we are calculating the integral on each element, we know that non-zero contributions can only come from a basis function whose index corresponds to one of the node indices of the element at hand and it is therefore better so have the sums over $k$ and $j$ above to only go over the nodes contained in that element. We then give each node another number for each element in which the node is contained. Hence, it is better to re-write the sum above as
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0a} = \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \left[ -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \hat{g}_z \right], \tag{5.64}
\end{equation}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0b} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \Bigg[ Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,ii)} \Bigg], \tag{5.65}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0c} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,kk)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,kk)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \Bigg], \tag{5.66}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0d} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \left[ -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} p_{l^p(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_{l^p(e,jj)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,ii)} \right], \tag{5.67}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1 \Bigg], \tag{5.68}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,2} &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_r^2 t_z^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_z^2 t_z^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} t_r^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_z^2 \partial_s \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} n_z^2 \Bigg], \tag{5.69}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,3} &= \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{n_{el}^3} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} \phi_{l_3(e_3,jj)} n_z^3 \phi_{l_3(e_3,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} t_z^3 \phi_{l_3(e_3,jj)} \phi_{l_3(e_3,ii)} \Bigg], \tag{5.70}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,4} &= \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{n_{el}^4} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} \phi_{l_4(e_4,jj)} n_z^4 \phi_{l_4(e_4,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} t_z^4 \phi_{l_4(e_4,jj)} \phi_{l_4(e_4,ii)} \Bigg]; \tag{5.71}
\end{align}
where double-letter indices are used to reference local node numbers, $n_v^e$ is the number of nodes where velocity is calculated in element $e$, $n_p^e$ is the number of nodes where pressure is calculated in element $e$, $n_v^{i,e_i}$ is the number of nodes where velocity is to be calculated on line element $e_i$ of boundary $i$, $l(e,jj)$ maps the local number $jj$ of a node in element $e$ to its global number, $l^p(e,jj)$ maps the local node number $jj$ of element $e$ to its pressure-node number, and similarly $l_k(e_k,jj)$ maps the local node number $jj$ of line-element $e_k$ in boundary $k$ to its global node number, and $l_k^k(e_k,jj)$ maps the local node number $jj$ of line-element $e_k$ on boundary $k$ to its boundary node number. Moreover, we have introduced functions $p_j^g$, $\sigma_j^1$, $\sigma_j^2$, $u_j^s$, $w_j^s$, $\lambda_j^2$, $\lambda_j^3$, $\gamma_j^3$, $\lambda_j^4$ and $\gamma_j^4$ whose index $j$ corresponds to a boundary numbering and are defined as the non-identically-null subset of the functions with the same name except for the tilde ($\tilde{\cdot}$) symbol. The same analogy applies to functions $l_k^k$. That is to say $\lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 = \tilde{\lambda}_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2$.
A form of optimisation that is similar to what was done with $j$ can be done in terms of index $i$. For a given index $i$, only the integrals on the elements that contain this node can have a non-zero contribution to the $i$-th residual. Hence, it is more convenient to loop over each element's nodes and find the contribution to $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ for each of the $i$s that are indices of the nodes in the element at hand, and to sum this contribution to each $\mathcal{M}_i^z$. We thus define
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0a} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \left[ -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \hat{g}_z \right], \tag{5.72}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0b} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \Bigg[ Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,ii)} \Bigg], \tag{5.73}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0c} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,kk)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,kk)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \Bigg], \tag{5.74}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,0d} &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{n_{el}} \left[ -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} p_{l^p(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_{l^p(e,jj)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,ii)} \right], \tag{5.75}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1 \Bigg], \tag{5.76}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,2} &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_r^2 t_z^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_z^2 t_z^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} t_r^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_z^2 \partial_s \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} n_z^2 \Bigg], \tag{5.77}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,3} &= \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{n_{el}^3} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} \phi_{l_3(e_3,jj)} n_z^3 \phi_{l_3(e_3,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} t_z^3 \phi_{l_3(e_3,jj)} \phi_{l_3(e_3,ii)} \Bigg], \tag{5.78}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,4} &= \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{n_{el}^4} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} \phi_{l_4(e_4,jj)} n_z^4 \phi_{l_4(e_4,ii)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} t_z^4 \phi_{l_4(e_4,jj)} \phi_{l_4(e_4,ii)} \Bigg]. \tag{5.79}
\end{align}
We can now re-write the $z$-momentum residual as
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0} + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.80}
\end{align}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^{z,1} &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca}, \tag{5.81}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} &= -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \hat{g}_z \equiv a_{ii,g_z}(e), \tag{5.82}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,jj}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,jj}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,jj}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,ii)} \equiv a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,ii)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,ii)} \equiv a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e), \tag{5.83}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,kk)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,kk)} \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\Omega_e} \phi_{l(e,ii)} \phi_{l(e,kk)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \equiv a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e), \tag{5.84}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} &= -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} p_{l^p(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_{l^p(e,jj)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,ii)} \equiv b_{jj,ii}^z(e), \tag{5.85}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_z^1 \partial_s \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1, \tag{5.86}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_r^2 t_z^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_z^2 t_z^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} t_r^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} t_z^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} t_z^2 \partial_s \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)} n_z^2, \tag{5.87}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} \phi_{l_3(e_3,jj)} n_z^3 \phi_{l_3(e_3,ii)} \equiv f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_3}^3} t_z^3 \phi_{l_3(e_3,jj)} \phi_{l_3(e_3,ii)} \equiv f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3), \tag{5.88}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} \phi_{l_4(e_4,jj)} n_z^4 \phi_{l_4(e_4,ii)} \equiv e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_4}^4} t_z^4 \phi_{l_4(e_4,jj)} \phi_{l_4(e_4,ii)} \equiv e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4). \tag{5.89}
\end{align}
Using the notation introduced above and re-arranging terms we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} = -\frac{2\dt St}{3} a_{ii,g_z}(e), \tag{5.90}
\end{equation}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \frac{2\dt}{3} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) + Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,jj}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,jj}(e) + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,jj}(e), \tag{5.91}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} Re\, w_{l(e,jj)} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left( u_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \left( r_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \left( z_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \Bigg], \tag{5.92}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} &= -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} p_{l^p(e,jj)} b_{jj,ii}^z(e), \tag{5.93}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \frac{1}{\ca} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii,t_z}(e_1) - p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right), \tag{5.94}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \Bigg[ \be \left( d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_r}(e_2) \{ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right. \nonumber\\
&\quad \left. + d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \{ w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) + \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{5.95}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) + \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \right), \tag{5.96}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) + \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \right). \tag{5.97}
\end{align}
Finally, we summarise the $z$-momentum residual as
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{e=1}^{n_{el}} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} + \sum_{e_1=1}^{n_{el}^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{j1},z_{j1}) \phi_i(r_{j1},z_{j1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{j1},z_{j1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{e_2=1}^{n_{el}^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{e_3=1}^{n_{el}^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{e_4=1}^{n_{el}^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.98}
\end{align}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} &= -\frac{2\dt St}{3} a_{ii,g_z}(e), \tag{5.99}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) + w_{l(e,jj)} \left( a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) + 2 a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \right) \right] \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} Re\, a_{ii,jj}(e) \left[ w_{l(e,jj)} - \frac{4}{3} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \right], \tag{5.100}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} Re\, w_{l(e,jj)} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left( u_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \left( r_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \left( z_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \Bigg], \tag{5.101}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} \frac{2\dt}{3} p_{l^p(e,jj)} b_{jj,ii}^z(e), \tag{5.102}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \frac{1}{\ca} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii,t_z}(e_1) - p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right), \tag{5.103}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \Bigg[ \be \left( d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_r}(e_2) \{ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right. \nonumber\\
&\quad \left. + d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \{ w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) + \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{5.104}
\end{align}
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) + \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \right), \tag{5.105}
\end{align}
and
\begin{align}
\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) + \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \right). \tag{5.106}
\end{align}

\subsection{Jacobian terms} % 5.1
We now calculate the derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $u_q$, $w_q$, $p_q$, $\sigma_q^1$, $\varepsilon_q^2$, $\varpi_q^2$, $\lambda_q^3$, $\gamma_q^3$, $\lambda_q^4$, $\gamma_q^4$ and $h_q$.

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $u_q$} % 5.1.1
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{u_q} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{u_q} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.107}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2}. \tag{5.108}
\end{equation}
Now, from equation (5.91) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) \partial_{u_q} u_{l(e,jj)} + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \frac{2\dt}{3} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} + Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}(e) \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}(e) \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}(e) \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}), \tag{5.109}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} = \frac{2\dt}{3} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)}. \tag{5.110}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.92) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} u_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e), \tag{5.111}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} = \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \big|_{q=l(e,kk)}. \tag{5.112}
\end{equation}
Finally from equation (5.95) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{u_q} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{u_q} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{u_q} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{u_q} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \partial_{u_q} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \partial_{u_q} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2, \tag{5.113}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} = \frac{2\dt \be}{3} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{5.114}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $w_q$} % 5.1.2
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{w_q} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{w_q} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.115}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2}. \tag{5.116}
\end{equation}
Now, from equation (5.91) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) \partial_{w_q} u_{l(e,jj)} + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \frac{2\dt}{3} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} + Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}(e) \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}(e) \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,jj}(e) \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}), \tag{5.117}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} = \frac{2\dt}{3} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} + \frac{4\dt}{3} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} + Re\, a_{ii,jj}(e) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)}, \tag{5.118}
\end{equation}
or, equivalently,
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} = \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( Re\, a_{ii,jj}(e) + a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) + 2 a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \right) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)}. \tag{5.119}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.92) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e), \tag{5.120}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} u_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,kk)} w_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} r_{l(e,kk)}^c a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} z_{l(e,kk)}^c a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \big|_{q=l(e,jj)} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e), \tag{5.121}
\end{align}
or, equivalently,
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{\substack{kk=1\\ q=l(e,jj)}}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{\substack{kk=1\\ q=l(e,jj)}}^{n_v^e} \left( u_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,kk)} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{\substack{kk=1\\ q=l(e,jj)}}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \left( r_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{\substack{kk=1\\ q=l(e,jj)}}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \left( z_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) - \frac{1}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \Bigg]. \tag{5.122}
\end{align}
Finally from equation (5.95) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{w_q} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{w_q} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{w_q} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{w_q} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \partial_{w_q} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \partial_{w_q} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2, \tag{5.123}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} = \frac{2\dt \be}{3} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{5.124}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $p_q$} % 5.1.3
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{p_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{p_q} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{p_q} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.125}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{p_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{p_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d}. \tag{5.126}
\end{equation}
Now, from equation (5.93), we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{p_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} = -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} b_{jj,ii}^z(e) \partial_{p_q} p_{l^p(e,jj)}, \tag{5.127}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{p_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} = -\frac{2\dt}{3} b_{jj,ii}^z(e) \big|_{q=l^p(e,jj)}. \tag{5.128}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\sigma_q^1$} % 5.1.4
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.129}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{align}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a), \tag{5.130}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \big|_{q=J1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \big|_{q=a}. \tag{5.131}
\end{align}
Now from equation (5.94) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1}\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{jj,ii,t_z}^s \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \partial_{\sigma_q^1} p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g, \tag{5.132}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1}\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} = \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} c_{jj,ii,t_z}^s \big|_{q=l_1(e_1,jj)}. \tag{5.133}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\varepsilon_q^2$} % 5.1.5
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.134}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2}. \tag{5.135}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.95) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2, \tag{5.136}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} = -\frac{\dt}{3\ca} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2^2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{5.137}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\varpi_q^2$} % 5.1.6
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\varpi_q^2}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.138}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\varpi_q^2}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2}. \tag{5.139}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.95) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\varpi_q^2}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varpi_q^2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varpi_q^2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varpi_q^2} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varpi_q^2} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \partial_{\varpi_q^2} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2, \tag{5.140}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\varpi_q^2}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} = \frac{2\dt}{3} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2^2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{5.141}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\lambda_q^3$} % 5.1.7
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\lambda_q^3}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
