&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.142}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\lambda_q^3}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3}. \tag{5.143}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.96) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\lambda_q^3}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \partial_{\lambda_q^3} \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3, \tag{5.144}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\lambda_q^3}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} = \frac{2\dt}{3} f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) \big|_{q=l_3(e_3,jj)}. \tag{5.145}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\gamma_q^3$} % 5.1.8
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\gamma_q^3}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.146}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\gamma_q^3}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3}. \tag{5.147}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.96) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\gamma_q^3}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \partial_{\gamma_q^3} \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3, \tag{5.148}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\gamma_q^3}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} = \frac{2\dt}{3} f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \big|_{q=l_3(e_3,jj)}. \tag{5.149}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\lambda_q^4$} % 5.1.9
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\lambda_q^4}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.150}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\lambda_q^4}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}. \tag{5.151}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.97) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\lambda_q^4}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \partial_{\lambda_q^4} \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4, \tag{5.152}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\lambda_q^4}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} = \frac{2\dt}{3} e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) \big|_{q=l_4(e_4,jj)}. \tag{5.153}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $\gamma_q^4$} % 5.1.10
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\gamma_q^4}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{J1},z_{J1}) \phi_i(r_{J1},z_{J1}) m_z^{1,n}(r_{J1},z_{J1})}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a) m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}, \tag{5.154}
\end{align}
which yields
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\gamma_q^4}\mathcal{M}_i^z = \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}. \tag{5.155}
\end{equation}
From equation (5.97) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\gamma_q^4}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \partial_{\gamma_q^4} \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4, \tag{5.156}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\gamma_q^4}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} = \frac{2\dt}{3} e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \big|_{q=l_4(e_4,jj)}. \tag{5.157}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{M}_i^z$ with respect to $h_q$} % 5.1.11
From equation (5.98) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_i^z &= \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} + \sum_{\substack{e=1\\ i=l(e,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^1} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_{j1},z_{j1}) \phi_i(r_{j1},z_{j1})}{\ca} \partial_{h_q} m_z^{1,n}(r_{j1},z_{j1}) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \frac{\sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \phi_i(r_a,z_a)}{\ca} \partial_{h_q} m_z^{1}(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^2} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} + \sum_{\substack{e_3=1\\ i=l_3(e_3,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^3} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} + \sum_{\substack{e_4=1\\ i=l_4(e_4,ii)}}^{\bar{n}_{el}^4} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4}. \tag{5.158}
\end{align}
From equation (5.90)
\begin{equation}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} = -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,g_z}(e), \tag{5.159}
\end{equation}
and passing to local spine numbers
\begin{equation}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0a} = -\frac{2\dt St}{3} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,g_z}(e) \big|_{q=S(e,qq)}. \tag{5.160}
\end{equation}
Now, from equation (5.91) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \frac{2\dt}{3} w_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) + Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}(e) + \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}(e), \tag{5.161}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \Bigg\{ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) + w_{l(e,jj)} \left( \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) + 2 \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \right) \right] \nonumber\\
&\quad + Re\, \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,jj}(e) \left[ w_{l(e,jj)} - \frac{4}{3} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \right] \Bigg\}, \tag{5.162}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0b} &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S(e,qq)}}^{n_v^e} \Bigg\{ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,jj}^{r,z}(e) \right. \nonumber\\
&\quad \left. + w_{l(e,jj)} \left( \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) + 2 \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e) \right) \right] \nonumber\\
&\quad + Re\, \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,jj}(e) \left[ w_{l(e,jj)} - \frac{4}{3} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} w_{l(e,jj)}(t_{n-2}) \right] \Bigg\}. \tag{5.163}
\end{align}
From equation (5.92) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} u_{l(e,kk)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,kk)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \partial_{h_q} r_{l(e,kk)}^c \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \partial_{h_q} z_{l(e,kk)}^c \nonumber\\
&\quad - Re \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{Re}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} w_{l(e,jj)} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e), \tag{5.164}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} Re\, w_{l(e,jj)} \Bigg\{ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left( u_{l(e,kk)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,kk)} \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \partial_{h_q} r_{l(e,kk)}^c + \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \left( r_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \right] \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \partial_{h_q} z_{l(e,kk)}^c + \partial_{h_q} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \left( z_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \right] \Bigg\}, \tag{5.165}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0c} &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S(e,qq)}}^{n_v^e} Re\, w_{l(e,jj)} \Bigg\{ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left( u_{l(e,kk)} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,kk)} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} r_{l(e,kk)}^c + \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,kk,jj}^r(e) \left( r_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} r_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \right] \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{kk=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} z_{l(e,kk)}^c + \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} a_{ii,kk,jj}^z(e) \left( z_{l(e,kk)}^c - \frac{4}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} z_{l(e,kk)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \right] \Bigg\}. \tag{5.166}
\end{align}
Now, from equation (5.93), we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} = -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_p^e} p_{l^p(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} b_{jj,ii}^z(e), \tag{5.167}
\end{equation}
and passing to local spine numbers we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e,ii}^{z,0d} = -\frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S(e,qq)}}^{n_p^e} p_{l^p(e,jj)} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} b_{jj,ii}^z(e). \tag{5.168}
\end{equation}
Now from equation (5.94) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \frac{2\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \partial_{h_q} c_{jj,ii,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1), \tag{5.169}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \frac{1}{\ca} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \partial_{h_q} c_{jj,ii,t_z}(e_1) - p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right), \tag{5.170}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_1,ii}^{z,1} &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S_1(e_1,qq)}}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( \frac{1}{\ca} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{jj,ii,t_z}(e_1) - p_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^g \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right). \tag{5.171}
\end{align}
From equation (5.95) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{2\dt \be}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{\dt}{3\ca} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2), \tag{5.172}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \Bigg[ \be \left( \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \{ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right. \nonumber\\
&\quad \left. + \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \{ w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) + \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{5.173}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_2,ii}^{z,2} &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S_2(e_2,qq)}}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \Bigg[ \be \left( \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,t_r,t_z}(e_2) \{ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right. \nonumber\\
&\quad \left. + \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,t_z,t_z}(e_2) \{ w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2\ca} \sigma_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,t_z}^s(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \lambda_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg]. \tag{5.174}
\end{align}
From equation (5.96) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \partial_{h_q} f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \partial_{h_q} f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3), \tag{5.175}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \partial_{h_q} f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) + \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \partial_{h_q} f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \right], \tag{5.176}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_3,ii}^{z,3} &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S_3(e_3,qq)}}^{n_v^{3,e_3}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ \lambda_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \partial_{h_{S_3(e_3,qq)}} f_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_3) + \gamma_{l_3(e_3,jj)}^3 \partial_{h_{S_3(e_3,qq)}} f_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_3) \right]. \tag{5.177}
\end{align}
From equation (5.97) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \partial_{h_q} e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \partial_{h_q} e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4), \tag{5.178}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \partial_{h_q} e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) + \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \partial_{h_q} e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \right], \tag{5.179}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q}\mathcal{M}_{e_4,ii}^{z,4} &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S_4(e_4,qq)}}^{n_v^{4,e_4}} \frac{2\dt}{3} \left[ \lambda_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \partial_{h_{S_4(e_4,qq)}} e_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_4) + \gamma_{l_4(e_4,jj)}^4 \partial_{h_{S_4(e_4,qq)}} e_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_4) \right]. \tag{5.180}
\end{align}

\section{The continuity equation} % 6
We consider
\begin{equation}
\partial_r u + \partial_z w = 0, \tag{6.1}
\end{equation}
and we define
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_r u + \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_z w, \tag{6.2}
\end{equation}
where $i$ is an index that runs through the pressure node numbering. Substituting approximations (4.66) and (4.67) we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_r \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j \right) + \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_z \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right), \tag{6.3}
\end{equation}
where $\mathcal{C}_i$ results from the substitution of the approximation of $u$ and $w$ into $\mathcal{C}_i$.
We can re-write this as
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_r \phi_j + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_z \phi_j, \tag{6.4}
\end{equation}
gathering the sums we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \left[ u_j \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_r \phi_j + w_j \int_{\Omega^f} \psi_i \partial_z \phi_j \right]. \tag{6.5}
\end{equation}
We now express the integrals as a sum over the integrals on each element
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \left[ u_j \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_i \partial_r \phi_j + w_j \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_i \partial_z \phi_j \right], \tag{6.6}
\end{equation}
where $n_{el,s}$ is the first element in the far field.
Moving to local numbering in variable $j$ we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_i \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} + w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_i \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \right]. \tag{6.7}
\end{equation}
Moving to local node numbers for index variable $i$ we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{C}_i &= \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_{l^p(e,ii)} \partial_r \phi_{l(e,jj)} \right. \nonumber\\
&\quad \left. + w_{l(e,jj)} \int_{\Omega_e} \psi_{l^p(e,ii)} \partial_z \phi_{l(e,jj)} \right], \tag{6.8}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii}, \tag{6.9}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{C}_{e,ii} = \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} b_{ii,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,jj)} b_{ii,jj}^z(e) \right]. \tag{6.10}
\end{equation}

\subsection{Jacobian terms} % 6.1
We now consider the derivatives of $\mathcal{C}_i$ with respect to $u_q$, $w_q$ and $h_q$.

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{C}_i$ with respect to $u_q$} % 6.1.1
From equation (6.9) we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii}, \tag{6.11}
\end{equation}
and from equation (6.10) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ b_{ii,jj}^r(e) \partial_{u_q} u_{l(e,jj)} + b_{ii,jj}^z(e) \partial_{u_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \right], \tag{6.12}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii} = b_{ii,jj}^r(e) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)}. \tag{6.13}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{C}_i$ with respect to $w_q$} % 6.1.2
From equation (6.9) we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii}, \tag{6.14}
\end{equation}
and from equation (6.10) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ b_{ii,jj}^r(e) \partial_{w_q} u_{l(e,jj)} + b_{ii,jj}^z(e) \partial_{w_q} w_{l(e,jj)} \right], \tag{6.15}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii} = b_{ii,jj}^z(e) \big|_{q=l(e,jj)}. \tag{6.16}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{C}_i$ with respect to $h_q$} % 6.1.3
From equation (6.9) we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{C}_i = \sum_{e=n_{el,s}}^{n_{el}} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii}, \tag{6.17}
\end{equation}
and from equation (6.10) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} b_{ii,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_q} b_{ii,jj}^z(e) \right], \tag{6.18}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{C}_{e,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^e} \left[ u_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} b_{ii,jj}^r(e) + w_{l(e,jj)} \partial_{h_{S(e,qq)}} b_{ii,jj}^z(e) \right]. \tag{6.19}
\end{align}

\section{The slip condition on the liquid-solid interface (SC2)} % 7
We recall equation (2.52)
\begin{equation}
\left( \mathbf{v}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} (\mathbf{u} + \mathbf{u}^s) \right) \cdot (\mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^2 \mathbf{n}^2) = E_s \nabla^s \varepsilon^2, \tag{7.1}
\end{equation}
and we define the $i$-th SC2 residual as
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 = \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \mathbf{v}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} (\mathbf{u} + \mathbf{u}^s) \right) \cdot \mathbf{t}^2 - E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \mathbf{t}^2 \cdot \nabla^s \varepsilon^2, \tag{7.2}
\end{equation}
which, of course we wish to make identically null.
We thus have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \mathbf{v}^{s2} \cdot \mathbf{t}^2 - \frac{1}{2} \mathbf{u} \cdot \mathbf{t}^2 - \frac{1}{2} \mathbf{u}^s \cdot \mathbf{t}^2 \right) - E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 (\partial_s \varepsilon^2) (\mathbf{t}^2 \cdot \mathbf{t}^2), \tag{7.3}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( u^{s2} t_r^2 + w^{s2} t_z^2 - \frac{1}{2} u t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} w t_z^2 - \frac{1}{2} u^s t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} w^s t_z^2 \right) - E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \partial_s \varepsilon^2, \tag{7.4}
\end{align}
equivalently
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u^{s2} t_r^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w^{s2} t_z^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u^s t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w^s t_z^2 - E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \partial_s \varepsilon^2, \tag{7.5}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u^{s2} t_r^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w^{s2} t_z^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u^s t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w^s t_z^2 - E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \partial_s \varepsilon^2. \tag{7.6}
\end{align}
We consider the last integral on the right hand side above and we integrate by parts to obtain
\begin{equation}
- \int_{\partial \Omega^{2}} \phi_i^2 \partial_s \varepsilon^2 = - \phi_i^2 \varepsilon^2 \Big|_{(r_c,z_c)}^{(r_o,z_o)} + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2}} \varepsilon^2 \partial_s \phi_i^2. \tag{7.7}
\end{equation}
This yields
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u^{s2} t_r^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w^{s2} t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 u^s t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 w^s t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \varepsilon^2 \partial_s \phi_i^2. \tag{7.8}
\end{align}
We recall the approximations
\begin{align}
u &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j, \tag{7.9} \\
w &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j, \tag{7.10} \\
\varepsilon^2 &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \varepsilon_j^2 \phi_j^2, \tag{7.11} \\
u^s &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^s \phi_j^2, \tag{7.12} \\
w^s &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^s \phi_j^2, \tag{7.13} \\
u^{s2} &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s2} \phi_j^2, \tag{7.14} \\
w^{s2} &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s2} \phi_j^2. \tag{7.15}
\end{align}
We thus have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s2} \phi_j^2 \right) t_r^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s2} \phi_j^2 \right) t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j^2 \right) t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j^2 \right) t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^s \phi_j^2 \right) t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^s \phi_j^2 \right) t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \varepsilon_j^2 \phi_j^2 \right) \partial_s \phi_i^2. \tag{7.16}
\end{align}
Moving the integrals into the sums, we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 t_r^2 + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 t_r^2 - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \varepsilon_j^2 \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,n}} \phi_j^2 \partial_s \phi_i^2. \tag{7.17}
\end{align}
Decomposing the integrals into sums over line elements and using local node numbers we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 = E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.18}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_r^2 + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_r^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_r^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \partial_s \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2, \tag{7.19}
\end{align}
where we have used the notation
\begin{align}
d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) &= \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_r^2, \tag{7.20} \\
d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) &= \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 t_z^2, \tag{7.21} \\
d_{ii,jj}^s(e_2) &= \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \partial_s \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2. \tag{7.22}
\end{align}
Thus,
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2). \tag{7.21}
\end{align}
Summarising and re-arranging terms we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{S}_i^2 = E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.22}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) \left( u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - \frac{1}{2} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \left( w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - \frac{1}{2} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2) \Bigg]. \tag{7.23}
\end{align}

\subsection{Jacobian terms} % 7.1
Here we find the derivative of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $u_q$, $w_q$, $u_q^{s2}$, $w_q^{s2}$, $\varepsilon_q^2$ and $h_q$.

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $u_q$} % 7.1.1
From equation (7.20)
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \partial_{u_q} \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \partial_{u_q} \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.24}
\end{align}
and from equation (7.21) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2), \tag{7.25}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 = -\frac{1}{2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{7.26}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $w_q$} % 7.1.2
From equation (7.20)
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \partial_{w_q} \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \partial_{w_q} \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.27}
\end{align}
and from equation (7.21) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2), \tag{7.28}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 = -\frac{1}{2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{7.29}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $u_q^{s2}$} % 7.1.3
From equation (7.20)
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \partial_{u_q^{s2}} \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \partial_{u_q^{s2}} \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.30}
\end{align}
and from equation (7.21) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2), \tag{7.31}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 = d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2^2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{7.32}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $w_q^{s2}$} % 7.1.4
From equation (7.20)
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \partial_{w_q^{s2}} \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \partial_{w_q^{s2}} \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.33}
\end{align}
and from equation (7.21) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2), \tag{7.34}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 = d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2^2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{7.35}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $\varepsilon_q^2$} % 7.1.5
From equation (7.20)
\begin{align}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.36}
\end{align}
and from equation (7.21) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2), \tag{7.37}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\varepsilon_q^2} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 = E_s d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2) \big|_{q=l_2^2(e_2,jj)}. \tag{7.38}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^2$ with respect to $h_q$} % 7.1.6
From equation (7.20)
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{S}_i^2 &= E_s \phi_i^2(r_c,z_c) \partial_{h_q} \varepsilon^2(r_c,z_c) - E_s \phi_i^2(r_o,z_o) \partial_{h_q} \varepsilon^2(r_o,z_o) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{h_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2, \tag{7.39}
\end{align}
and from equation (7.21) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) - \frac{1}{2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_q} d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2), \tag{7.40}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) \left( u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - \frac{1}{2} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \partial_{h_q} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \left( w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - \frac{1}{2} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_q} d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{7.41}
\end{align}
and passing to local spine numbers
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_2,ii}^2 &= \sum_{\substack{jj=1\\ q=S_2(e_2,qq)}}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_2) \left( u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - \frac{1}{2} u_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_2) \left( w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - \frac{1}{2} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)} - \frac{1}{2} w_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + E_s \varepsilon_{l_2^2(e_2,jj)}^2 \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{jj,ii}^s(e_2) \Bigg]. \tag{7.41}
\end{align}

\section{Impermeability condition (I2)} % 8
We recall equation (2.51) which states
\begin{equation}
\left( \mathbf{v}^{s2} - \mathbf{u}^s \right) \cdot \mathbf{n}^2 = 0, \tag{8.1}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
(u^{s2} - u^s) n_r^2 + (w^{s2} - w^s) n_z^2 = 0, \tag{8.2}
\end{equation}
where $\mathbf{v}^{s2} = (u^{s2}, w^{s2})$, and we define the $i$-th residual of the impermeability equation as
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_i &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 u^{s2} n_r^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 w^{s2} n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 u^s n_r^2 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 w^s n_z^2, \tag{8.3}
\end{align}
where $i$ is an index that runs through the boundary 2 node numbering.
We recall the approximations given by
\begin{align}
u^s &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^s \phi_j^2, \tag{8.4} \\
w^s &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^s \phi_j^2, \tag{8.5}
\end{align}
and we introduce
\begin{align}
u^{s2} &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s2} \phi_j^2, \tag{8.6} \\
w^{s2} &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s2} \phi_j^2. \tag{8.7}
\end{align}
Using these, we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_i &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s2} \phi_j^2 \right) n_r^2 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s2} \phi_j^2 \right) n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^s \phi_j^2 \right) n_r^2 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^s \phi_j^2 \right) n_z^2, \tag{8.8}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_r^2 + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_r^2 - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_z^2, \tag{8.9}
\end{align}
gathering the sums we obtain
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \Bigg[ u_j^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_r^2 + w_j^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_r^2 - w_j^s \int_{\partial \Omega^{2,f}} \phi_i^2 \phi_j^2 n_z^2 \Bigg]. \tag{8.10}
\end{align}
Now, we decompose the integrals into the sum of the integrals over each line-element on boundary 2
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{I}_i = \sum_{e_2=1}^{n_{el}^2} \mathcal{I}_{e_2,ii}, \tag{8.11}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_{e_2,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_r^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_z^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_r^2 \nonumber\\
&\quad - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_z^2 \Bigg], \tag{8.12}
\end{align}
and expressing sums over index $j$ in terms of local node numbers we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_{e_2,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg( u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_r^2}_{d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_z^2}_{d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_r^2}_{d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_2}^2} \phi_{l_2(e_2,ii)}^2 \phi_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^2 n_z^2}_{d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2)} \Bigg), \tag{8.13}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_{e_2,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg( u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg). \tag{8.14}
\end{align}
Summarising and re-arranging we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{I}_i = \sum_{e_2=1}^{n_{el}^2} \mathcal{I}_{e_2,ii}, \tag{8.15}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{I}_{e_2,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg( d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) \left[ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \right] \nonumber\\
&\quad + d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \left[ w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \right] \Bigg). \tag{8.16}
\end{align}

\subsection{Jacobian terms} % 8.1
We now calculate the derivatives of $\mathcal{I}_i$ with respect to $u_q^{s2}$, $w_q^{s2}$ and $h_q$.

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{I}_i$ with respect to $u_q^{s2}$} % 8.1.1
We consider
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{8.17}
\end{align}
passing the derivative into the sum we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{I}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{u_q^{s2}} u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) \Big|_{q=l_2(e_2,jj)}, \tag{8.18}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q^{s2}} \mathcal{I}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2). \tag{8.19}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{I}_i$ with respect to $w_q^{s2}$} % 8.1.2
We consider
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{8.20}
\end{align}
passing the derivative into the sum we have
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{I}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{w_q^{s2}} w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Big|_{q=l_2(e_2,jj)}, \tag{8.21}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q^{s2}} \mathcal{I}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2). \tag{8.22}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{I}_i$ with respect to $h_q$} % 8.1.3
From equation (8.14) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)}}^{n_{el}^2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \partial_{h_q} \Bigg[ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg]. \tag{8.23}
\end{align}
Passing to local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)\\ q=S_2(e_2,qq)}}^{n_{el}^2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad + w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \nonumber\\
&\quad - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \Bigg], \tag{8.24}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{I}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_2=1\\ i=l_2(e_2,ii)\\ q=S_2(e_2,qq)}}^{n_{el}^2} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{2,e_2}} \Bigg[ \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_2) \left( u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - u_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \partial_{h_{S_2(e_2,qq)}} d_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_2) \left( w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^{s2} - w_{l_2(e_2,jj)}^s \right) \Bigg]. \tag{8.25}
\end{align}

\section{The slip condition equation on boundary 1 (SC1)} % 12
We recall equation (2.47), which states
\begin{equation}
\left( \mathbf{v}^{s1} - \mathbf{u} \right) \cdot \left( \mathbf{I} - \mathbf{n}^1 \mathbf{n}^1 \right) = \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \nabla^s \sigma^1. \tag{12.1}
\end{equation}
We define the $i$-th SC1 residual as
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 (\mathbf{v}^{s1} - \mathbf{u}) \cdot \mathbf{t}^1 - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 \mathbf{t}^1 \cdot \nabla^s \sigma^1, \tag{12.2}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 \mathbf{v}^{s1} \cdot \mathbf{t}^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 \mathbf{u} \cdot \mathbf{t}^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 (\partial_s \sigma^1) \mathbf{t}^1 \cdot \mathbf{t}^1, \tag{12.3}
\end{align}
equivalently
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 u^{s1} t_r^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 w^{s1} t_z^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 u t_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 w t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 \partial_s \sigma^1. \tag{12.4}
\end{align}
We consider the last integral on the right hand side above and we integrate by parts to obtain
\begin{equation}
- \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,\ell}} \phi_i^1 \partial_s \sigma^1 = - \phi_i^1 \sigma^1 \Big|_{(r_j,z_j)}^{(r_a,z_a)} + \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i^1. \tag{12.5}
\end{equation}
This yields
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 u^{s1} t_r^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 w^{s1} t_z^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 u t_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 w t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \sigma^1 \partial_s \phi_i^1 + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_j,z_j) \sigma^1(r_j,z_j) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \sigma^1(r_a,z_a). \tag{12.6}
\end{align}
We now recall the approximations
\begin{align}
u &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j, \tag{12.7} \\
w &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j, \tag{12.8} \\
\sigma^1 &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \sigma_j^1 \phi_j, \tag{12.9}
\end{align}
and we introduce
\begin{align}
u^{s1} &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s1} \phi_j, \tag{12.10} \\
w^{s1} &\approx \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s1} \phi_j. \tag{12.11}
\end{align}
Substituting these approximations into the residual equation we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s1} \phi_j \right) t_r^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s1} \phi_j \right) t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \phi_j \right) t_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \phi_j \right) t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \sigma_j^1 \phi_j \right) \partial_s \phi_i^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \sigma^1(r_a,z_a). \tag{12.12}
\end{align}
Moving the integrals into the sum we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 t_r^1 + \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 t_r^1 - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 t_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} \sigma_j^1 \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_j^1 \partial_s \phi_i^1. \tag{12.13}
\end{align}
Decomposing the integral into sums over line-elements and passing to local node numbers we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1, \tag{12.14}
\end{align}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_r^1}_{c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_z^1}_{c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_r^1}_{c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1)} \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 t_z^1}_{c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1)} \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \underbrace{\int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \partial_s \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1}_{c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1)}, \tag{12.15}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1). \tag{12.16}
\end{align}
Summarising and re-arranging terms we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1, \tag{12.17}
\end{align}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \Bigg[ c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} - u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \left( w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} - w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1) \Bigg]. \tag{12.18}
\end{align}

\subsection{Jacobian terms} % 12.1
Here we find the derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $u_q$, $w_q$, $u_q^{s1}$, $w_q^{s1}$, $\sigma_q^1$ and $h_q$.

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $u_q$} % 12.1.1
Using equation (12.14) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \partial_{u_q} \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \partial_{u_q} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1. \tag{12.19}
\end{align}
From equation (12.16) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \partial_{u_q} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1), \tag{12.20}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 = - c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \big|_{q=l_1(e_1,jj)}. \tag{12.21}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $w_q$} % 12.1.2
Using equation (12.14) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \partial_{w_q} \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \partial_{w_q} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1. \tag{12.22}
\end{align}
From equation (12.16) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \partial_{w_q} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1), \tag{12.23}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 = - c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \big|_{q=l_1(e_1,jj)}. \tag{12.24}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $u_q^{s1}$} % 12.1.3
Using equation (12.14) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \partial_{u_q^{s1}} \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \partial_{u_q^{s1}} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1. \tag{12.25}
\end{align}
From equation (12.16) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q^{s1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q^{s1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \partial_{u_q^{s1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q^{s1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q^{s1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1), \tag{12.26}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 = c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \big|_{q=l_1(e_1,jj)}. \tag{12.27}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $w_q^{s1}$} % 12.1.4
Using equation (12.14) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \partial_{w_q^{s1}} \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \partial_{w_q^{s1}} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1. \tag{12.28}
\end{align}
From equation (12.16) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q^{s1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q^{s1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \partial_{w_q^{s1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q^{s1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q^{s1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1), \tag{12.29}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 = c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \big|_{q=l_1(e_1,jj)}. \tag{12.30}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $\sigma_q^1$} % 12.1.5
Using equation (12.14) and local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)\\ q=S_1(e_1,qq)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1. \tag{12.31}
\end{align}
From equation (12.16) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{\sigma_q^1} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1) \partial_{\sigma_q^1} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1, \tag{12.32}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{\sigma_q^1} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 = \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1) \big|_{q=l_1(e_1,jj)}. \tag{12.33}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{S}_i^1$ with respect to $h_q$} % 12.1.6
Using equation (12.14) and local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{S}_i^1 &= \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_c,z_c) \partial_{h_q} \sigma^1(r_c,z_c) - \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \phi_i^1(r_a,z_a) \partial_{h_q} \sigma^1(r_a,z_a) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)\\ q=S_1(e_1,qq)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1. \tag{12.34}
\end{align}
From equation (12.16) we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1), \tag{12.35}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} \mathcal{S}_{e_1,ii}^1 &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \Bigg[ \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,t_r}(e_1) \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} - u_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,t_z}(e_1) \left( w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} - w_{l_1(e_1,jj)} \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{1 + 4 E_g B_g}{4 B_g} \sigma_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{jj,ii}^s(e_1) \Bigg]. \tag{12.36}
\end{align}

\section{Kinematic boundary condition (KBC)} % 13
We consider equation (2.44) which states
\begin{equation}
(\mathbf{v}^{s1} - \mathbf{c}) \cdot \mathbf{n}^1 = 0, \tag{13.1}
\end{equation}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
u^{s1} n_r^1 - u^c n_r^1 + w^{s1} n_z^1 - w^c n_z^1 = 0, \tag{13.2}
\end{equation}
and define
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{K}_i = \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i^1 u^{s1} n_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i^1 u^c n_r^1 + \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i^1 w^{s1} n_z^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1,f}} \phi_i^1 w^c n_z^1, \tag{13.3}
\end{equation}
where $i$ is an index that runs on the boundary 1 numbering of the free surface nodes.
We substitute approximations (4.54) and (4.55) and obtain
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_i &= \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 u^{s1} n_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \frac{3 r^c(t_n) - 4 r^c(t_{n-1}) + r^c(t_{n-2})}{2 \dt} n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 w^{s1} n_z^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \frac{3 z^c(t_n) - 4 z^c(t_{n-1}) + z^c(t_{n-2})}{2 \dt} n_z^1, \tag{13.4}
\end{align}
multiplying by $2\dt/3$ we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_i &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 u^{s1} n_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 r^c n_r^1 + \frac{4}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 r^c(t_{n-1}) n_r^1 - \frac{1}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 r^c(t_{n-2}) n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 w^{s1} n_z^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 z^c n_z^1 + \frac{4}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 z^c(t_{n-1}) n_z^1 - \frac{1}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 z^c(t_{n-2}) n_z^1, \tag{13.5}
\end{align}
We substitute approximations (4.66)-(4.69) into the equation above and obtain
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_i &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s1} \phi_j^1 \right) n_r^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c \phi_j^1 \right) n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c(t_{n-1}) \phi_j^1 \right) n_r^1 - \frac{1}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c(t_{n-2}) \phi_j^1 \right) n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s1} \phi_j^1 \right) n_z^1 - \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c \phi_j^1 \right) n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c(t_{n-1}) \phi_j^1 \right) n_z^1 - \frac{1}{3} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \left( \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c(t_{n-2}) \phi_j^1 \right) n_z^1. \tag{13.6}
\end{align}
Moving the integrals into the sums we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_i &= \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 - \frac{1}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 - \frac{1}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\partial \Omega^{1}} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1. \tag{13.7}
\end{align}
Now, we decompose the integrals into the sum of the integrals over each line-element on boundary 1
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{e_1=1}^{n_{el}^1} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} u_j^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 - \frac{1}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} r_j^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} w_j^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 - \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 - \frac{1}{3} \sum_{j=1}^{n_v} z_j^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_i^1 \phi_j^1 n_z^1 \Bigg]. \tag{13.8}
\end{align}
Re-writing we have
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_r^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1 \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \int_{\partial \Omega_{e_1}^1} \phi_{l_1(e_1,ii)}^1 \phi_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^1 n_z^1 \Bigg]. \tag{13.11}
\end{align}
Re-arranging we have
\begin{equation}
\mathcal{K}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \mathcal{K}_{e_1,ii}, \tag{13.12}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\mathcal{K}_{e_1,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \Bigg[ c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \left( \frac{2\dt}{3} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} - r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c + \frac{4}{3} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) - \frac{1}{3} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \left( \frac{2\dt}{3} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} - z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c + \frac{4}{3} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) - \frac{1}{3} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \Bigg]. \tag{13.13}
\end{align}

\subsection{Jacobian terms} % 13.1
We now calculate the derivatives of $\mathcal{K}_i$ with respect to $u_q^{s1}$, $w_q^{s1}$ and $h_q$.

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{K}_i$ with respect to $u_q^{s1}$} % 13.1.1
We consider (13.11), from where we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{u_q^{s1}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \Bigg], \tag{13.14}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \partial_{u_q^{s1}} u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1}, \tag{13.15}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{u_q^{s1}} \mathcal{K}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)\\ q=l_1(e_1,jj)}}^{n_{el}^1} \frac{2\dt}{3} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1). \tag{13.16}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{K}_i$ with respect to $w_q^{s1}$} % 13.1.2
We consider (13.13), from where we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{w_q^{s1}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \Bigg], \tag{13.17}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \frac{2\dt}{3} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \partial_{w_q^{s1}} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1}, \tag{13.18}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{w_q^{s1}} \mathcal{K}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)\\ q=l_1(e_1,jj)}}^{n_{el}^1} \frac{2\dt}{3} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1). \tag{13.19}
\end{equation}

\subsubsection{Derivatives of $\mathcal{K}_i$ with respect to $h_q$} % 13.1.3
We consider (13.13), from where we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \partial_{h_q} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \Bigg], \tag{13.20}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)}}^{n_{el}^1} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_q} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \partial_{h_q} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c - c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \partial_{h_q} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \Bigg], \tag{13.21}
\end{align}
and using local spine numbers we have
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{K}_i &= \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)\\ q=S_1(e_1,qq)}}^{n_{el}^1} \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} \left( u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{4}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - \frac{1}{3} \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) + z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad - c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c - c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \Bigg], \tag{13.22}
\end{align}
i.e.
\begin{equation}
\partial_{h_q} \mathcal{K}_i = \sum_{\substack{e_1=1\\ i=l_1(e_1,ii)\\ q=S_1(e_1,qq)}}^{n_{el}^1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} \mathcal{K}_{e_1,ii}, \tag{13.23}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} \mathcal{K}_{e_1,ii} &= \sum_{jj=1}^{n_v^{1,e_1}} \Bigg[ \frac{2\dt}{3} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \nonumber\\
&\quad - \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_r}(e_1) \left( r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c - \frac{4}{3} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} r_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \nonumber\\
&\quad + \frac{2\dt}{3} w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^{s1} \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \nonumber\\
&\quad - c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \nonumber\\
&\quad - z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c \partial_{h_{S_1(e_1,qq)}} c_{ii,jj,n_z}(e_1) \left( z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c - \frac{4}{3} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-1}) + \frac{1}{3} z_{l_1(e_1,jj)}^c(t_{n-2}) \right) \Bigg]. \tag{13.24}
\end{align}

\section{Summary of residual equations}
\subsection{Bulk terms}
\subsection{r-momentum residuals}

\begin{equation}
\begin{array}{r l}
\hat{M}_{i}^{r} = \sum_{e = 1}^{n_{e1}}\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{r} + \sum_{e = 1}^{n_{e1}^{1}}\hat{M}_{e_{1},ii}^{r,1} + \sum_{i = l_{2}(e_{2},ii)}^{n_{e2}^{2}}\hat{M}_{e_{2},ii}^{r,2} \\
\qquad +\sum_{e = 1}^{n_{e3}^{3}}\hat{M}_{e_{3},ii}^{r,3} + \frac{\sigma_{1}^{4}\phi_{i}(r_{d},z_{d}) - \sigma_{e}^{1}\phi_{i}(r_{c},0)\cos(\theta)}{C a},
\end{array} \tag{17.1}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{r} &= \sum_{j = 1}^{n_{v}}\left(u_{l(e,jj)}\left\{Re\sum_{k = 1}^{n_{v}}\left[u_{l(e,kk)}a_{ii,kk,jj}^{r}(e) + w_{l(e,kk)}a_{ii,kk,jj}^{2}(e)\right]\right.\right. \nonumber\\
&\qquad \left.\left. + 2a_{ii,jj}^{r,r}(e) + a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e)\right\} +w_{l(e,jj)}a_{ii,jj}^{z,z}(e)\right) \nonumber\\
&\qquad -\sum_{j = 1}^{n_{v}^{e}}p_{l\nu (e,jj)}b_{jj,ii}^{r}(e), \tag{17.2}\\
\hat{M}_{e_{1},ii}^{r,1} &= \frac{1}{C a}\sum_{j = 1}^{n_{v}}\sigma_{l_{1}(e_{1},jj)}^{1}c_{ir,jj,ii}^{z}(e_{1}), \tag{17.3}\\
\hat{M}_{e_{2},ii}^{r,2} &= Be\left\{\sum_{j = 1}^{n_{v}}\left[u_{l_{2}(e_{2},jj)}d_{t_{r},t_{r},ii,jj}(e_{2}) + w_{l_{2}(e_{2},jj)}d_{t_{r},t_{2},ii,jj}(e_{2})\right] + d_{t_{r},t_{r},ii}(e_{2})\right\}, \tag{17.4}\\
\hat{M}_{e_{3},ii}^{r,3} &= \sum_{j = 1}^{n_{v}^{e3}}\left[\lambda_{l_{3}^{3}(e_{3},jj)}^{3}f_{ii,jj,n_{r}}(e_{3}) + \gamma_{l_{3}^{3}(e_{3},jj)}^{3}f_{t_{r},ii,jj}(e_{3})\right]. \tag{17.5}
\end{align}

\subsection{z-momentum residuals}
\begin{equation}
\hat{M}_i^z = \sum_{e = 1}^{n_{cl}}\hat{M}_{e,ii}^z +\sum_{e = 1}^{n_{cl}^1}\hat{M}_{e,ii}^z +\sum_{e = 1}^{n_{cl}^{2}}\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{z,2} \tag{17.6}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{align}
\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{z} &= \sum_{j = 1}^{n_{e}^{c}}\left\{w_{l(e,jj)}\left\{Re\sum_{kk = 1}^{n_{e}^{c}}\left[w_{l(e,kk)}a_{ii,kk,jj}^{r}(e) + w_{l(e,kk)}a_{ii,kk,jj}^{z}(e)\right] + 2a_{ii,ij}^{z,z}(e)\right\} \right\} \tag{17.7}\\
\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{z,1} &= \frac{1}{Ca}\sum_{j = 1}^{n_{e}^{c1}}\sigma_{l_{1}(e_{1},jj)}^{1}c_{t_{2},jj,ii}^{z}(e_{1}), \tag{17.8}\\
\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{z,2} &= Be\left\{\sum_{j = 1}^{n_{e}^{2},e_{2}}\left[w_{l_{2}(e_{2},jj)}d_{t_{r},t_{r},ii,jj}(e_{2}) + w_{l_{2}(e_{2},jj)}d_{t_{r},t_{2},ii,jj}(e_{2})\right]\right\} \tag{17.9}\\
\hat{M}_{e,ii}^{z,3} &= \sum_{j = 1}^{n_{e}^{3}}\gamma_{l_{3}(e_{3},jj)}^{3}f_{t_{r},ii,jj}(e). \tag{17.10}
\end{align}

\subsection{Continuity residuals}
\begin{equation}
\hat{C}_i = \sum_{e = 1}^{n_{e1}}\sum_{i = 1}^{n_e^e}\left[u_{l(e,ii)}b_{jj,ii}^e (e) + w_{l(e,ii)}b_{jj,ii}^e (e_3)\right]. \tag{17.11}
\end{equation}

\subsection{Kinematic boundary condition residuals}
\begin{equation}
\hat{K}_i = \sum_{e_1 = 1}^{n_{e1}^1}\sum_{j,j = 1}^{n_{e1}^e}\left[u_{l_1(e_1,jj)}c_{ii,jj,n_e}(e_1) + w_{l_1(e_1,jj)}c_{ii,jj,n_e}(e_{1})\right]. \tag{17.12}
\end{equation}

\subsection{Impermeability residuals}
\begin{equation}
